### Post by jimbolad on 2013-08-30
Hello,

As you will probably figure out i am very new to ubuntu and linux. I have recently bought a new ultrabook (samsung series 5 NP530U3C-A09UK) :

it has a 500GB HDD + 24 GB Express Cache SSD...

Whilst on windows 8 i created the boot usb drive and had to change a few BIOS settings in order for it to work and then eventually I got to the ubuntu installation.

When installing, It gave me a choice of the 500GB hardrive or the 24GB SSD, I chose the SSD thinking it would load quicker and boot quicker etc. any way I am now very confused

as ubuntu is now showing an 18GB drive shown below

### Post by oldfred on 2013-08-30
UltraBooks have UEFI vs BIOS (you want UEFI), Intel SRT (you need to remove RAID meta-data) and dual video issues (can you set one or the other?).
More info on UEFI and Ultrabook issues in the link in my signature.

Other Samsungs, should be similar:
 Samsung Ultrabook Windows 8 & Ubuntu & recovery boot Disk view of partitions post 7
[http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2097690](http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2097690)
Samsung Series 7 - post #5 Windows 8 & UEFI, Ubuntu only to new SSD
[http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?p=12382951](http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?p=12382951)
 SAMSUNG Series 3 NP365E5C-XXXXX laptops 
[http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2120763](http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2120763)
Samsung series 5 UltraBook, erase Windows & install to SSD
[http://schoolsplay.wordpress.com/2012/11/22/install-ubuntu-linux-on-a-samsung-series-5-ultrabook-with-ssd/](http://schoolsplay.wordpress.com/2012/11/22/install-ubuntu-linux-on-a-samsung-series-5-ultrabook-with-ssd/)
